 & {\em itr} & -\/ the iterator to the table row containing the record to retrieve. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}

\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}

\end{DoxyPostcond}

\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx128\+\_\+lowerbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a896515137d9a7844105786ee3a6b1d47}{uint128\+\_\+t}}, 16 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary 128-\/bit integer index table that matches the lowerbound condition for a given secondary key. Lowerbound secondary index is the first secondary index which key is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= the given secondary index key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ pointer to secondary key first used to determine the lowerbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}secondary} will be replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. 

If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx128\+\_\+upperbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a896515137d9a7844105786ee3a6b1d47}{uint128\+\_\+t}}, 16 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary 128-\/bit integer index table that matches the upperbound condition for a given secondary key. The table row that matches the upperbound condition is the first table row in the table with the lowest secondary key that is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} the given key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ pointer to secondary key first used to determine the upperbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Find a table row in a secondary 256-\/bit integer index table by primary key.

256-\/ 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em data} & -\/ pointer to the array of 2 {\ttfamily uint128\+\_\+t} integers which will act as the buffer to hold the retrieved secondary key of the found table row. \\

 & {\em primary} & -\/ the primary key of the table row to look up.\\
\hline

\end{DoxyPostcond}

Find the table row in a secondary 256-\/bit integer index table that matches the lowerbound condition for a given secondary key. Lowerbound secondary index is the first secondary index which key is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= the given secondary index key.

256-\/

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a14b47d476fa0049575494cd970d8f8e2} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx256\+\_\+next (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}}}]{iterator}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}} $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row following the referenced table row in a secondary 256-\/bit integer index table.

256-\/ 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em iterator} & -\/ the iterator to the referenced table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the next table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the table row following the referenced table row (or the end iterator of the table if the referenced table row is the last one in the table). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
{\ttfamily iterator} points to an existing table row in the table. 
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
{\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the table row following the referenced table row if it exists, otherwise {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be left untouched. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx256\+\_\+previous (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}}}]{iterator}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}} $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row preceding the referenced table row in a secondary 256-\/bit integer index table.

256-\/ 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em iterator} & -\/ the iterator to the referenced table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the previous table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the table row preceding the referenced table row assuming one exists (it will return -\/1 if the referenced table row is the first one in the table). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
{\ttfamily iterator} points to an existing table row in the table or it is the end iterator of the table. 
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
{\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the table row preceding the referenced table row if it exists, otherwise {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be left untouched. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\index{db\_idx256\_upperbound@{db\_idx256\_upperbound}!sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{db\_idx256\_upperbound()}{db\_idx256\_upperbound()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a16740dd30d90ef2997a998e9fb47f692} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx256\+\_\+upperbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a2058365f8ef9bc59b7205f8b8c0aab50}{legacy\+\_\+span}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a896515137d9a7844105786ee3a6b1d47}{uint128\+\_\+t}}, 16 $>$}]{data}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary 256-\/bit integer index table that matches the upperbound condition for a given secondary key. The table row that matches the upperbound condition is the first table row in the table with the lowest secondary key that is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} the given key.

256-\/ 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em data} & -\/ pointer to the secondary key data (which is stored as an array of 2 {\ttfamily uint128\+\_\+t} integers) first used to determine the upperbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, the buffer pointed to by {\ttfamily data} will be filled with the secondary key of the found table row. 

If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

Find a table row in a secondary 64-\/bit integer index table by secondary key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
 & {\em secondary} & -\/ the pointer to the secondary index key. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a \textquotesingle{}uint64\+\_\+t\textquotesingle{} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the first table row with a secondary key equal to {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}secondary} or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a0b47faf1af7ab73f3a88c3d3aa6ba535} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx64\+\_\+lowerbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary 64-\/bit integer index table that matches the lowerbound condition for a given secondary key. Lowerbound secondary index is the first secondary index which key is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= the given secondary index key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ pointer to secondary key first used to determine the lowerbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}secondary} will be replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. 

If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx64\+\_\+upperbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary 64-\/bit integer index table that matches the upperbound condition for a given secondary key. The table row that matches the upperbound condition is the first table row in the table with the lowest secondary key that is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} the given key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ pointer to secondary key first used to determine the upperbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{db\_idx\_double\_upperbound@{db\_idx\_double\_upperbound}!sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{db\_idx\_double\_upperbound()}{db\_idx\_double\_upperbound()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a56b65f39056ce49fd0955fc1e7e10cec} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx\+\_\+double\+\_\+upperbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structfloat64__t}{float64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary double-\/precision floating-\/point index table that matches the upperbound condition for a given secondary key. The table row that matches the upperbound condition is the first table row in the table with the lowest secondary key that is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} the given key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ pointer to secondary key first used to determine the upperbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, the buffer pointed to by {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}secondary} will be filled with the secondary key of the found table row. 

If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx\+\_\+long\+\_\+double\+\_\+lowerbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structfloat128__t}{float128\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary quadruple-\/precision floating-\/point index table that matches the lowerbound condition for a given secondary key. Lowerbound secondary index is the first secondary index which key is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= the given secondary index key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ Pointer to secondary key first used to determine the lowerbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}secondary} will be replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. 

If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{db\_idx\_long\_double\_upperbound()}{db\_idx\_long\_double\_upperbound()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_aee276cb7bb8d8f42f4fc60ba83a1f2b3} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+idx\+\_\+long\+\_\+double\+\_\+upperbound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structfloat128__t}{float128\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{secondary}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_adaac58ba7cbf7caade7008a8778c2464}{legacy\+\_\+ptr}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}, 8 $>$}]{primary}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a secondary quadruple-\/precision floating-\/point index table that matches the upperbound condition for a given secondary key. The table row that matches the upperbound condition is the first table row in the table with the lowest secondary key that is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} the given key.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
 & {\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
 & {\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em secondary} & -\/ pointer to secondary key first used to determine the upperbound and which is then replaced with the secondary key of the found table row. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em primary} & -\/ pointer to a {\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t} variable which will have its value set to the primary key of the found table row.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the found table row or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
If and only if the table row is found, the buffer pointed to by {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}secondary} will be filled with the secondary key of the found table row. 

If and only if the table row is found, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}primary} will be replaced with the primary key of the found table row. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

Find the table row in a primary 64-\/bit integer index table that matches the lowerbound condition for a given primary key. Lowerbound record is the first nearest record which primary key is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= the given key.

\end{DoxyParams}

Find the table row following the referenced table row in a primary 64-\/bit integer index table.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em itr} & -\/ the iterator to the referenced table row. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyPostcond}

\Hypertarget{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a784e21d384b7cfe02a9632215e83dce8}\index{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}!db\_update\_i64@{db\_update\_i64}}
\index{db\_update\_i64@{db\_update\_i64}!sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{db\_update\_i64()}{db\_update\_i64()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a784e21d384b7cfe02a9632215e83dce8} 
void sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+update\+\_\+i64 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}}}]{itr}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{payer}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a2058365f8ef9bc59b7205f8b8c0aab50}{legacy\+\_\+span}}$<$ const char $>$}]{buffer}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Update a record in a primary 64-\/bit integer index table.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em itr} & -\/ iterator to the table row containing the record to update. \\
\hline
{\em payer} & -\/ the account that pays for the storage costs. \\
\hline
{\em buffer} & -\/ new updated record.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This function does not allow changing the primary key of a table row. The serialized data that is stored in the table row of a primary table may include a primary key and that primary key value could be changed by the contract calling the db\+\_\+update\+\_\+i64 intrinsic; but that does not change the actual primary key of the table row.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
{\ttfamily itr} points to an existing table row in the table. 
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
the record contained in the table row pointed to by {\ttfamily itr} is replaced with the new updated record. 
\end{DoxyPostcond}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a715074eb64d60b0e5d55e323b2345639} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_ab1967d8591af1a4e48c37fd2b0f184d0}{int32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::db\+\_\+upperbound\+\_\+i64 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{code}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{scope}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{table}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_aec6fcb673ff035718c238c8c9d544c47}{uint64\+\_\+t}}}]{id}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find the table row in a primary 64-\/bit integer index table that matches the upperbound condition for a given primary key. The table row that matches the upperbound condition is the first table row in the table with the lowest primary key that is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} the given key.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em code} & -\/ the name of the owner of the table. \\
\hline
{\em scope} & -\/ the scope where the table resides. \\
\hline
{\em table} & -\/ the table name. \\
\hline
{\em id} & -\/ the primary key used as a pivot to determine the upperbound record.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
iterator to the upperbound record or the end iterator of the table if the table row could not be found. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Retrieves the code hash for an account, if any.

struct \{ varuint32 struct\+\_\+version; uint64\+\_\+t code\+\_\+sequence; \doxylink{classfc_1_1sha256}{fc\+::sha256} code\+\_\+hash; uint8\+\_\+t vm\+\_\+type; uint8\+\_\+t vm\+\_\+version; \} result;

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_aa8725e5c597dcc71a3e57f601607642d}\index{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}!get\_parameters\_packed@{get\_parameters\_packed}}
\index{get\_parameters\_packed@{get\_parameters\_packed}!sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_parameters\_packed()}{get\_parameters\_packed()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_aa8725e5c597dcc71a3e57f601607642d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a435d1572bf3f880d55459d9805097f62}{uint32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::get\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+packed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a68ee5032824b9877df35eec12344398d}{span}}$<$ const char $>$}]{packed\+\_\+parameter\+\_\+ids}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a68ee5032824b9877df35eec12344398d}{span}}$<$ char $>$}]{packed\+\_\+parameters}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Retrieve the blockchain config parameters. The input buffer is a packed data stream which represents an encoded sequence of parameter\+\_\+id pairs with the following format\+: \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}varuint32\+:sequence\+\_\+length \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} varuint32\+:parameter\+\_\+id \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} ... The output buffer is a packed data stream which represents an encoded sequence of parameter\+\_\+id\+:paramter\+\_\+value pairs with the following format\+: \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}varuint32\+:sequence\+\_\+length \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} varuint32\+:parameter\+\_\+id \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} $<$various$>$\+:parameter\+\_\+value \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} ... The encoding of parameter\+\_\+values should be specific to the parameter being set The output buffer format should be valid input for set\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+packed. For each known parameter\+\_\+id in the input sequence there should be an associated entry in the output sequence with the current encoded parameter\+\_\+value.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em packed\+\_\+parameter\+\_\+ids} & -\/ the input buffer with the format as described above. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em packed\+\_\+parameters} & -\/ the output buffer with the format as described above. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{get\_wasm\_parameters\_packed@{get\_wasm\_parameters\_packed}!sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_wasm\_parameters\_packed()}{get\_wasm\_parameters\_packed()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a90f227ea255f8735c3ef8fd081775ef4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a435d1572bf3f880d55459d9805097f62}{uint32\+\_\+t}} sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::get\+\_\+wasm\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+packed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a68ee5032824b9877df35eec12344398d}{span}}$<$ char $>$}]{packed\+\_\+parameters}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{stdint_8h_a435d1572bf3f880d55459d9805097f62}{uint32\+\_\+t}}}]{max\+\_\+version}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Get the current wasm limits configuration.

The structure of the parameters is as follows\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item max\+\_\+mutable\+\_\+global\+\_\+bytes The maximum total size (in bytes) used for mutable globals. i32 and f32 consume 4 bytes and i64 and f64 consume 8 bytes. Const globals are not included in this count.
\item max\+\_\+table\+\_\+elements The maximum number of elements of a table.
\item max\+\_\+section\+\_\+elements The maximum number of elements in each section.
\item max\+\_\+linear\+\_\+memory\+\_\+init The size (in bytes) of the range of memory that may be initialized. \doxylink{struct_data}{Data} segments may use the range \mbox{[}0, max\+\_\+linear\+\_\+memory\+\_\+init).
\item max\+\_\+func\+\_\+local\+\_\+bytes The maximum total size (in bytes) used by parameters and local variables in a function.
\item max\+\_\+nested\+\_\+structures The maximum nesting depth of structured control instructions. The function itself is included in this count.
\item max\+\_\+symbol\+\_\+bytes The maximum size (in bytes) of names used for import and export.
\item max\+\_\+module\+\_\+bytes The maximum total size (in bytes) of a wasm module.
\item max\+\_\+code\+\_\+bytes The maximum size (in bytes) of each function body.
\item max\+\_\+pages The maximum number of 64 KiB pages of linear memory that a contract can use. Enforced when an action is executed. The initial size of linear memory is also checked at setcode.
\item max\+\_\+call\+\_\+depth The maximum number of functions that may be on the stack. Enforced when an action is executed.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em packed\+\_\+parameters} & the ouput for the parameters. \\
\hline
 & {\em max\+\_\+version} & has no effect, but should be 0.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the size of the packed parameters if packed\+\_\+parameters is empty, otherwise it returns the amount of data written in packed\+\_\+parameters. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{privileged_8cpp_source_l00085}{85}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{privileged_8cpp_source}{privileged.\+cpp}}.

Big integer modular exponentiation

$<$\+BASE$>$ $<$\+EXPONENT$>$ $<$\+MODULUS$>$ returns an output (BASE\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+EXPONENT) \% MODULUS as a byte array \{\{\{\{ with the same length as the modulus \}\}\}\}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & -\/ the result (BASE\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+EXPONENT) \% MODULUS \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1 if there was an error 0 otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a6fe0029c6e0ed6e35310c3936e1849b6}\index{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}!set\_parameters\_packed@{set\_parameters\_packed}}
\index{set\_parameters\_packed@{set\_parameters\_packed}!sysio::chain::webassembly::interface@{sysio::chain::webassembly::interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_parameters\_packed()}{set\_parameters\_packed()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classsysio_1_1chain_1_1webassembly_1_1interface_a6fe0029c6e0ed6e35310c3936e1849b6} 
void sysio\+::chain\+::webassembly\+::interface\+::set\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+packed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a68ee5032824b9877df35eec12344398d}{span}}$<$ const char $>$}]{packed\+\_\+parameters}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the blockchain parameters. It allows a system contract the ability to set parameters in a flexible manner. The input buffer is a packed data stream which represents an encoded sequence of parameter\+\_\+id\+:paramter\+\_\+value pairs with the following format\+: \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}varuint32\+:sequence\+\_\+length \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} varuint32\+:parameter\+\_\+id \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} $<$various$>$\+:parameter\+\_\+value \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} ... The encoding of parameter\+\_\+values should be specific to the parameter being set. Having duplicate parameter\+\_\+ids encoded in the sequence should result in aborting the transaction context. The presence of a parameter\+\_\+id which is unknown OR which is known but tied to an unactivated consensus protocol should result in aborting the transaction context. There are no requirement for the ordering of items in the sequence.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em packed\+\_\+parameters} & -\/ buffer to hold the packed data with the format described above. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
